ASALINSU

a duk lokacin da nainah xata koma skul idan taje tasha xata shiga mota takesamun baffanta tsaye yana jiranta saboda inna bata bari yaba nainah komai sai gyadar dayake noma _can you imagine yanda xaa tura yaro boarding ba abinci ba kudi sai gyada fisabilillah_
autana Allah ya kaiki lfy ya dawo dake lfy kici gaba da addua kinji
ta share hawayen fuskarta tana kallonsator baffa
yaciro kudi dari biyu tsohuwa dunqule jikinsa har rawa yake yace gashi auta kinsan banda kudi bana aikin komai sai noma da zarar nasami kudi xn aikomaki kinji

tace anty bahijja ta boyemin maqota kada inna tagani ta amshe shine yau da safe tabani
ya share yawayensa yana sanyawa majeed albarka a xuciyarsa xaije yayi masa godiya ya qara jaddadamasa indai yana raye nainah tasashe matarsace halaq malaq

*MUS'AB* ya fito daga xuriar Alhaji Mohd kaita shine kadai yaronsa a duniya bayan matan,yanada mata daya Mufida da yar'su Sulaimi wacce nainah ke raino watanta goma tana koyon tfy ayanxu
Matashine mai shekara 27,idan kaganshi ma baxakace yanada aure ba yarone sosai Mahaifinsa yayi masa aure da 25 ganin kansa ba wuri daya ba game da mata sannan yanason yaronsa da tarbiya bayason ya lalace da rayuwar mata shiyasa yayi mass auren wuri ko ince auren gata da mufida diyar qanwarsa
mus'ab bayason auren amma ya karba dan bai iya musu da mahaifinsa sai dai bayason halin mufida ko kadan batada nutsuwa tafiye tsiwa ga kuri ga shegen son jiki komai sai kai aiki ko wurin shimfida bata tabuka komai haka xai qare bidirinsa yaaa tsaki cike da takaici yatashi batare da ya gamsuba,sannan gatada mugun kishin tsiya ko masu aikinta bata bari sugansh tana kafkaf dasui kada a kwacemata shi ko friends dinta da yawa basu sanshiba
wasu kuma a pics kawai suka sanshi ko gidan sukazo indai yana gidan hankalinta baya kwantawa har saitayi masa magana ya fita ta falonsa,xai fice yana girgixa kansa fuskarsa dauke da

Cikakken matashi dan shekara ashirin da bakwai yanada wata irin halitta da kalar fat mai daukar hankali da fisgo xuciya daga garesa musamman daga fitinannun matan da sukasan qirar namijin duniya,
dogone wankan tarwada mai ginannan jinkin da babu qiba babu rama a jikinsa,kamannin uwa da ubane suka cakude suka bada surar wannan giant mai sanya xuciyar diya mace cikin soyayya ta babu gaira babu dalili,idanunsa kadai suna narkarda xuciyar yan mata shiyasa mufida take kaffa kaffa da abinta batason kowacce mace ta rabi jikin mijinta

NAINAH - 11-15 - Wattpad
Sauri take tana qarawa tana tafe Tana share hawayen fuskarta saboda dukan da Inna tayimata safiyar yau Dan kawai ta makara bata tashi da wuri ba, gashi kuma tayi lattin xuwa wurin aikinta, 
Tafiyar minti talatin tayi a qafa kafin ta qarasa gidan, flat ne hawa daya Wanda aka gina da red bricks wato Jan bulo,irin tsarin gidajen ingila furanni sunyi yawa gidan, rumfa daga sama hr qasa sannan ga springs na bubbugowa daga cikin dutse
Tana shiga cikin falon ta ci Karo da mufida fuskarta a murtuqe, gabanta yayi mummunan faduwa ta durqusa qasa tana fadin Anty ina kwana? Tace Ke Nainah karki maidani wata shashasha aiki na daukeki Idan baxaki iya bane Ki gayamin na sallameki akwai mutane da yawa dake neman aikin
Idanun Nainah sukayi rau rau hawaye fal a idonta Tace kiyi haquri Anty baxan qara makara ba dan Allah Ki yafemin 
Taja tsaki Tana fadin ku talakawan nan kamar gareku aka somajin kalmar haquri, ta juya, Nainah tace Anty ina sulaimi? 
Tana gun mahaifinta idan ya gama wasa da ita xn kawo maki ita kuma Ki fitar min daga falo tun mijina bai fito ba, 
Da sauri Nainah tabar falon, mufida taja dogon tsaki hannuwanta a qugunta tana kallonta hrta fice tana jin haushin Nainah sosai ba dan komai ba sai dan kyawunta, 
Duk da yarinyar na cikin talauci da rashin samun kulawa kyawunta bai taba gushewa ba, kasancewarta buxuwa take da fari sosai kamar Ja, tana da manyan idanuwa da dogon hanci, bakinta dan qaramine jawur dashi kamar tasa jan baki amma haka halittarsa take, gashinta shine yafi daukar hankali, ga tsawo ga cika kuma baqi sosai, lokacin da mufida taga gashin Nainah sai da ta tsorata, bama mufida ba hr Inna tsoron gashinta take, shiyasa mufida Ke kishin Nainah sosai hrtake kwankwanto anya ba aljana bace ita komai tanada? 
Bahijja ma haka take sai dai Nainah tafita gashi da hasken fata sosai, yasir ma da yake namiji daka ganshi kasan ciki daya suka fito dasu Nainah suna da kamanni sosai na mahaifiyarsu hrdai Nainah
Bayan fitowar Nainah ta nufi inda masu aikin gidan ke xama, ta gaidasu kafin ta sami guri ta xauna, hajjo yar dattijuwa tana cikin masu girki ta matso kusa da Nainah
Yar'nan mai ya hana maki xuwa da wuri hajiya na ta fada? Nainah ta janyo hannun tsohuwar suka matsa daga gefe Tana girmama tsohuwar dn tana sonta sosai, 
Tace hajjo kinga yau ma Inna tayimin duka ta hanamin Karin safe dan kawai na makara ban tashi da wuri ba, Ya Yaye mata bayanta duk yayi shatin bulala rudu-rudu abinka da farin mutum duk bayanta yayi jawur, hajjo ta girgixa kanta cike da takaici 
Tace kiyi haquri Nainah kibarta da Allah haqqinku Dana mahaifinku ma Ya isheta ganin isharar duniya, Ki daina kukan haka idanunki sunyi jawur, Nainah ta share hawayen fuskarta da gefen dan kwalinta, Hajjo tace waina na nan na ajiye maki xo muje kici, ta juya Nainah nabi bayanta cike da qaunar tsohuwar, 
Ta matsa kadan daga su ige dake gyaran kifi ta xauna ta soma ci suna hira sama sama cos batason surutu ko kadan, bata dauki wani lokaci sosai ba ta cinye tas, hajjo taxo da ruwa a bokiti 
Tace taso Nainah tun aiki baiyi yawa ba na wanke maki Wannan Kan, tubarakallah gaki da gashi hr baya bakya gyaransa ynxu fa ke kin girma kin xama budurwa yakamata ace kina tsabtace jikinki, 
Nainah ta tashi Tana warware tubkar gashin kanta wnda da kyar bahijja ta iya daure mata shi, Duk wurin suka Xuba mata idanu kowa da abinda yake saqawa a xuciyarsa game da gashin, ta tsugunna hajjo ta wanke shi fes sai sheqi yakeyi, 
Tace kije dakinmu damuke kwana akwai toilet aciki kiyi wanka Ki taje kan Ki shafeshi da mai, 
Tace hajjo bnda kayan sanyawa Tace akwai towel aciki Ki daura, kisanya hijabina na wanke maki kayan Idan sun bushe ki sanya kafin akawo maki raino

] Pherty: Nainah kallon tsohuwar take, itace mutum ta biyu bayan majeed dake nuna mata qauna haka, da hanxari taje tacire ta dauro towel bayan ta xumbula qaton hijabi hr qasa taxo ta kawo wa hajjo Kayan
Ya fito dauke da sulaimi daga part dinsa Ya nufi part din mufida bata nan Ya nufi Dakinta bata nan, jin motsin ruwa a toilet Ya tabbatar masa tana ciki tana wanka, 
Ya juya Ya nufi part din masu aiki dauke da sulaimi akayi sa'a Duk suna kitchen suwaiba ce kawai Ke wanke wankeYace keee ina mai rainon sulaimi? Jikinta na rawa ta nuna masa dakin da Nainah take ciki, yaja dogon tsaki Ya nufi dakin ita kuma Tabishi da kallo Tana fadi a ranta ashe haka yake da kyawu shiyasa hjy bata bari muganshi? 
Batare da tunanin komai ba Ya fada dakin da sallama, Nainah na tsaye tana taje kanta duk Ya xubo bayanta, towel ne ajikinta jin sallamar namiji Ya sanyata qin juyowa sai dai ta amsa Sallamar qasan maqoshinta Wanda ba lallai bane Ya jiyo, 
Shi kuma mutuwar tsaye yayi jikinsa hr rawa yake saboda tsabar rudewa da ganin gashinta, Duk matan da yake gani bai taba ganin mai irin gashinnan ba, bugu da qari hasken fatarta Ya qara Jan hankalinsa, 
Jin shiru a xaton ta kowaye Ya fita ya sanyata juyowa idanunta na sauka akan yatsun qafafunsa sai ta juya da Sauri batare data Kalli fuskarsa ba, hankalinta a tashe ko waye miye dalilinsa na tsayuwa bayanta? Jikinta na soma rawa kamar daga sama taji muryarsa mai sanyin gske yana fadinGa sulaimi nan, ya ajiyeta a saman gado Ya juya da Sauri Ya fice xuciyarsa na harbawa, 
Sai da taji bugawar qofa sannan ta sauke ajiyar xuciya ta juyo tana kallon sulaimi, aikuwa tana ganinta ta wangale baki tana dariya Tana tsalle hade da miqo mata hannu alamar ta dauketa

Nainah xaune da umma lotee qanwar mamanta, tana kuka take gaya mata komai an kwace mata saurayi an bawa bahijja sannan an aura mata mai mata wanda bata so, 
Ran Lotee Ya baci sosai musamman ynda Nainah Ke mata kukan a raba aurensu ita bata so, 
'kayi shiru Nainah kagayamin shi Wancan yaro da aka bawa bahijja kana sonsa ne, (bata iya Hausa sosai ba)
'umma ni bana sonsa ynxu nadaina sonsa Duk bana sonsu karatuna nakeso, ynxu fa S

3 xnje,
'Tor shikenan Nainah amma bai kamata Nasir Ya maku haka ba Kodan yaga mahaifiyarku bata Raye xai riqa maku dole ga masu kudi, ya manta kuna da naku dangi ne?

'tun da bakaso baxaka koma ba dole ya aiko maka takardarki ko kuma yazo Ya baki ni xan kwatar maka yan'cin ki,
Nagode umma Lotee
Tun da ta kwanta ta kasa samun nutsuwa Idan ta rufe idanuwanta Mus'ab take gani, cutie face dinsa take gani, murmushinsa ,da idanunsa daya Ke tsare ta da kallo dasu, ta tashi xurum tana kallon lotee dake barci, ta tuna Idan yana kallonta Yanda take xare masa ido, 'hey friend why are you looking at me? Ta saki murmushi, ta tuna Idan tana cin abinci yakan xauna yayi ta kallonta, da'a gidane da ynxu suna tare komai tace yayi xai mata komai tasa shi xaiyi yana murna,oh missing you friend, but why na kasa barci sai tunaninka, ta dafe goshinta
'Oh God, tunanin majeed bai taba hanamin barci ba sai naka? Why? You are just a friend to me, thinking of you will not stop me from leaving you
Lotee Ta gyara kwanciyarta idanunta na sauka akan Nainah dake xaune, a hankali ta kira sunanta,Nainah! Ta juyo tana kallonta batare da ta amsa ba, 'me kake a xaune cikin duhu, me Ya hana maka barci? 
'kaina Ke ciwo umma, Lotee Ta Kunna fitilar dakin tana kallonta,batayi Kama da mai Ciwon kai ba, 'ko kana tunanin mijinkine? Ta xare ido sosai'nooo umma why should I? 'ni bajin turanci nake ba kamin Hausa ko yare na, Nainah ta kwanta tana fadin'umma bana tunaninsa, amma inajin gabana na faduwa tun daxu ina tsoron wani abu ya sami baffa ko yayi fushi dani bayan nazo
'Ki kwantarda hankalinka baxai maki komai ba
Olryt Nyt Umma
Mtsew ta kashe fitilar cike da takaicin turancin da Nainah keyi,yaran xamani ma akwai rainin wayo
Washe gari hakama ta tashi sukuku ta tuna irin Wannan lokacin xai xo Ya tsareta, 'Nainah kinci abinci, me kikeso, me zan sa akawo maki, Xakici tare dani sai tace a'ah, tor kici *haskena*, Idan kin gama ni xanje naci nawa, haka xai tsareta hr sai ta gama kana Ya fita, yau gata tana kalaci da madarar shanu da kekena, Bamai rarrashinta, ko ba komai yana sanyata murmushi da Nishadi,yana da kyau numfashinsa yana da qamshi, ta saki murmushi caraf suka hada ido da Latee,'kai Wannan yaro munafikin yaro ne, tun daxu ina mgn kana can kana tuna Wancan miji naka kuma kace baka sonsa,yanxu ka xauna kana tunaninsa, 
'kai umma bashi nake tunani ba, believe me bana sonsa just thinking about him Kingane
Tor ka gama shan Wannan kekeni kaxo zan aikeka inda kawun ka
Kusan azahar Nainah ta dawo dauke da Kaya akanta a gajiye take Duk inda Tabi maza da mata kallonta suke sunga baquwar fuska sunga mai Kama da Yaren su banbanci fatar Nainah tafi kyau da sheqi da Alama Hutu ne da yanayin wurin xama, da haka ta qaraso gidan bakinta a tunxure cike da takaicin kallon da suke mata, 
Tana shigo wa gidan taja ta tsaya curus, xuciyarta na buga sakamakon ganin Mus'ab, Majeed da Bahijja xaune tare da Lotee,
Lokaci daya suka Juyo suna kallonta idanunsu suka sarqe dana juna ita da Mus'ab, atare xuciyoyinsu na soma bugawa, tayi Saurin dauke idanuwanta ta daga qafafuwanta da kyar tayi shigewarta daki batare da ta sake kallonsu ko yi masu magana ba

Cikin muryar damuwa ya soma mgn

Umma tace na sani ynxu na fahimci kana so yarona da kyau kana damuwa dashi shi kuma yaxo ya gayamin qarya akanka harnace xan raba aurenku, tunda kana sonta haka baxan rabaka da matarka ba kuma zan Baka daki ka xauna har Ayi Bikin bahijja, Karka damu da munafikin yarona ai naganshi Jiya baiyi barci ba, su bahijja suka soma dariya, Nainah na bakin qofa tana kallonsu, Lotee taja hannunsa takaishi wani daki, ba komai aciki sai gadon karfe irin Wannan mai rumfar sama, a qasa an malalen wurin da Tabarma ga jere irin nasu na buxayen nijar, sunyi ado da kwarya mai xane mai kyau anjera an Qawata dakin, jeren dakin har sama yayi tsawo, dakin Ya birgeshi in his life bai taba xaton akwai daki irin haka da mutane xasu iya rayuwa acikin Saba, hassalima bai taba xaton xai iya shigowa acikinsa Ballantana ya kwana aciki ba
